  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_da13759a-faed-47f4-a559-3e7507e62584'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer6804599222586033276">Obsession, defined as the domination of one's thoughts or feelings by a persistent idea, image or desire....<br/><br/>Chantel Rosenberg's passion for music and life had never shone brighter than the time she spent in Bordeaux France.   <span id="freeText6804599222586033276" style="display:none">Obsession, defined as the domination of one's thoughts or feelings by a persistent idea, image or desire....<br /><br />Chantel Rosenberg's passion for music and life had never shone brighter than the time she spent in Bordeaux France. It's a time when feelings arose and desires ran deep, a time that fundamentally changed her life.<br /><br />A man living in seclusion, Phillipe Tibideau is haunted and plagued by memories he cannot disregard. Choosing to live a quiet life in his Chateau surrounded by the vineyards of France, he's left his passion for art behind. <br /><br />However, the time has arrived to tell his side of a tale. A tale that has depicted him as a 'beautiful monster' and he's finally allowing someone close.<br /> <br />Close enough to ask questions. Questions he's not sure he wants to answer. Questions about her.<br /><br />For up and coming journalist Gemma Harris, the pursuit of truth is what drives her and when a job of a lifetime presents itself there is nothing in the world that will stop her from taking it. Even if it does mean leaving her home for several months to stay at Chateau Tibideau, with him.<br /><br />This is a story of what happens when three passionate lovers collide and the desire for truth, art and music merge.<br /><br />Chateau Tibideau is a place full of unanswered questions, dark sinful desire and a beauty so hauntingly sad it will have you wondering how you will ever leave the same....</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9716862766876718127"><b>5 obsessive stars.*****Review completed March 28, 2013</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776324.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mjuxpmMm3I1qffcrao8_500_zps3df4d3df.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdus."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776325.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mjuxpmMm3I1qffcrao5_500_zps66dbd0d6.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>Reporter Gemma Harris arrives at Château Tibideau in Bordeaux, France, to meet the world-renowned artist, Phillipe Tibideau. Besides, he’s stopped producing wine and didn’t want to paint </span>
  <span id="freeText9716862766876718127" style="display:none"><b>5 obsessive stars.*****Review completed March 28, 2013</b><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776324.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjuxpmMm3I1qffcrao8_500_zps3df4d3df.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdus."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776325.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mjuxpmMm3I1qffcrao5_500_zps66dbd0d6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Reporter Gemma Harris arrives at Château Tibideau in Bordeaux, France, to meet the world-renowned artist, Phillipe Tibideau. He was once one of the most public and famous faces in the world, however, since a couple of months the critically acclaimed artist lives in seclusion and shies away from media and visitors. Besides, he’s stopped producing wine and didn’t want to paint anymore. Now Gemma is here to tell Phillipe’s mysterious tale because he invited her to his château. He is <i>the</i> man who will either make or break her career. From the beginning Gemma feels drawn to Phillipe, his expressive art, as well as his fascinating yet somber aura. Though she knows there is more to it than meets the eye.<br> <br><blockquote>

Both women gave me the impression of a symbiosis, even though it’s hard to compete with someone who has already left. Also, the journal entries are not only complementing the story, they are a very substantial and intriguing part of <i>Blind Obsession,</i> as is the book title which is very apt.         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer506409857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15046344879576419274"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405149i/788899.jpg' alt=' photo chantelfholesdiva_zps45b91a39.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Before you embark on this one, you should know that this is very different from Ella Franks’ contemporary romances. This is her first foray into erotica and it’s not strictly a love story. There is love to be found here but it won’t make you happy, beautiful as it is – in fact, I think it will break your heart.<br/><br/>This is possibly THE most atmospheric piece of erotica that I think I have ever read. It’s sublimely sensual, devastatingly emotional and so stunningly erotic that it’s entirely possibly t</span>
  <span id="freeText15046344879576419274" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405149i/788899.jpg" alt=" photo chantelfholesdiva_zps45b91a39.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before you embark on this one, you should know that this is very different from Ella Franks’ contemporary romances. This is her first foray into erotica and it’s not strictly a love story. There is love to be found here but it won’t make you happy, beautiful as it is – in fact, I think it will break your heart.<br><br>This is possibly THE most atmospheric piece of erotica that I think I have ever read. It’s sublimely sensual, devastatingly emotional and so stunningly erotic that it’s entirely possibly to lose oneself entirely in this novel. It’s also ‘interactive’ but I’ll leave that for you to find out exactly what that entails for when you read the book yourself.<br><br>I think it’s very important not to spoil the story so I’ll just give you the bare bones. Philippe is a reclusive erotic artist hiding away in his chateau in France. He’s created a series of paintings featuring his muse and his love, Chantel Rosenberg. He’s been vilified in the press over what happened in the past and now he’s decided to invite up and coming journalist Gemma Harris to spend some time at the Chateau and to finally to tell the story from his own point of view with the aid of Chantel’s journals. So this story is told entirely by Philippe, Gemma and the voice of Chantel in the past through her journals. It leads to an incredibly insular feel to the whole novel and adds immeasurably to the incredible atmosphere.<br><br>At first I thought this had a Beauty &amp; The Beast vibe but, even though Philippe has locked himself away due to his self-perceived guilt, he really is no Beast. Then, it felt a little like Interview With The Vampire, itself an incredibly atmospheric novel and also I felt strong similarities to Daphne du Maurier’s Rebecca but, in the end, all comparisons fell away and this novel now stands all by itself – there are no comparisons and this is completely unforgettable.<br><br>The story, while beautifully erotic, is pervaded by an air of sadness that never leaves you. It’s mournful, melancholy, and incredibly sombre. It all begins and ends with Chantel Rosenberg. Philippe may now be holding and caressing Gemma but he never lets go of Chantel. I felt the desperate need to reach into the novel and yell at Gemma to get out while she still could – I wanted to tell her "he doesn’t love you, he doesn’t even see you – he sees only Chantel" but, of course, it’s not possible and we’re dragged along the heart-breaking journey that this novel takes right along with Gemma.<br><br>And I grew to despise Philippe for his actions, for his emotional cruelty to Gemma. His story, once told, is so very devastating that it’s hard to despise him for long, hard not to feel intense sympathy for him but there were moments when I wanted to inflict serious pain on him.<br><br>Gemma, to me, was like an invisible heroine – we learned virtually nothing about her as she became consumed by Philippe and Chantel’s heart-breaking story and slowly began to re-enact it. She’s completely overshadowed by the events of the past and is now so immersed in them that she’s losing herself, becoming fully wrapped up in Philippe &amp; Chantel’s story and is slowly and irrevocably headed towards emotional disaster.<br><br>To say more would be to spoil the plot and it needs to be experienced without any prior knowledge. You don’t need to know what to expect, you just need to read and feel, to go on the sensual ride with Gemma, to experience it as she did and to lose yourself, just as she did.<br><br>So, for a first foray into erotica, this is highly accomplished yet also so heartrending. Ella Frank is an incredibly talented writer, her style is engaging and captivating and she’s always written powerfully erotic sex scenes, never more so than in Blind Obsession. This book made me angry, it also completely broke my heart and I will never, NEVER forget it.<br><br>4.5 unforgettable stars<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405149i/788900._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo chateautibideauquote_zpsbfe7dae7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of Ella Frank<br><br>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>

<div id="review_587972334" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/587972334" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/587972334?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=2013-release">2013-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=swoonworthy-male-lead">swoonworthy-male-lead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587972334" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10760042032612696200"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdu."<br/>It means; "True paradises are paradises we have lost."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412193ra/810504.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Hauntingly beautiful...</i>
</b><br/><br/>Those are the two words I would use to best describe <i>Blind Obsession</i>. From the moment I started reading this story it managed to captivate my entire attention. It was an intense, powerful and enthralling story and I enjoyed reading every second of it.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Blind Obsession</i>
</b> is a story about love, passion, trust, beauty, art and music bound together in an</span>
  <span id="freeText10760042032612696200" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdu."<br>It means; "True paradises are paradises we have lost."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380412193ra/810504.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><b>
  <i>Hauntingly beautiful...</i>
</b><br><br>Those are the two words I would use to best describe <i>Blind Obsession</i>. From the moment I started reading this story it managed to captivate my entire attention. It was an intense, powerful and enthralling story and I enjoyed reading every second of it.<br><br><b>
  <i>Blind Obsession</i>
</b> is a story about love, passion, trust, beauty, art and music bound together in an enticing and irresistible mixture that left me speechless and blown away after reading it.<br><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br><br><i>"In wine country in Bordeaux, France, I met a man.<br>Yes, today out in wine country, I met a man, and something about that man moved me.<br>Something about that man changed me."</i> ~ Chantel<br><br>She met a man named <b>Phillipe Tibideau --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379800126i/664434._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is a true artist. Once upon a time, not so long ago, he was acclaimed and praised all over the world for his brilliant work.<br><br>His artwork includes a series of paintings that have been revered as <i>
  <b>"an alluring mixture of dark eroticism enhanced now by its devastatingly haunting sadness."</b>
</i><br><br>He used to be one of the most popular faces around the world. But now, he is a man so private and so isolated from the outside world that no one has seen or heard from him in months.<br><br>All because of the tragic events that happened, in and around his chateau in France, <i>Chateau Tibideau.</i><br><br>Now, he is a man, haunted by his past...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417291i/825159.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The world blames him for what happened during those tragic events. They depicted him as a "beautiful monster".<br><br>For months, Phillipe has kept himself quiet about what truly happened but now, finally, the time has come for Phillipe to tell <i>his side</i> of the story...<br><br>Therefore,he has invited a journalist <b>Gemma Harris --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417291i/825160._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He has invited her to his chateau in France where she will stay for a few months to write the story of a lifetime.<br><br>She will tell the world not only his story, but <i>their</i> story. The story of Phillipe and Chantel. The story behind his world renowned series of paintings called <i>Blind Obsession</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"What inspired you to paint your critically acclaimed series?"<br><br>"Beauty." There's a pregnant pause before he repeats himself louder. "Beauty inspired me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Beauty is Chantel...</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417291i/825161.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Chantel Rosenberg</b> is the woman behind the paintings. She's a blind woman but her disability has never kept her from developing her talent and becoming a very successful violin player.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>She became Phillipe's muse and foremost important source of inspiration behind the paintings. She became not only his muse, but also the love of his life. Or better yet, the obsession of his life...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I love you. That is the beginning and that is the end. That is everything."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417291i/825162._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For Gemma, the opportunity has come to unravel the history of what happened between these two lovers.<br><br>Gemma is a strong, independent woman, purposefully chosen to be the objective eye to Phillipe and Chantel's stoty. But soon, she finds herself becoming not only captivated by the mysterious, tortured yet brilliantly talented artist that is Phillipe Tibideau; she also becomes more and more enthralled by the very detailed writing in Chantel's journal. Those journal entries in the book really give the reader a important and vividly described recapitulation of everything that happened between Phillipe in Chantel, through Chantel's eyes.<br><br>After a few interview sessions, Phillipe decides, the best way for Gemma to experience what is was like to be his muse, is for her to pose in the exact same nude poses, Chantel posed in. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I think for you to understand this story, you must first become a part of it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Although Gemma in so way resembles Chantel - in fact she's more like her complete opposite - Phillipe finds himself drawn to her in the same way he was drawn to <i>her</i>. Chantel still consumes all of his thoughts, but through his sexual seduction of Gemma, he finds himself being drawn to her more and more.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"When I was inside of her, nothing else existed," he confesses. "And when I'm inside of you, she's starting not to exist."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417291ra/825163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417291ra/825164.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Right now, you're mine, just like <i>she</i> was mine. I'm going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can't forget."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/578264.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>The sex scenes were sensually written and scorching hot! Some of the hottest ones I have ever read. But even during those scenes, it's always about more than just sex, it's about this deep, powerful connection between two people who are drawn to each other in an undeniable and all-consuming way.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>"I'd heard about people falling in love, and I'd heard about lust. What I had never heard of was this all-consuming need to be inside another human being. I felt this desperate compulsion to become one with him. This was desire. This was to crave. This was what it felt like to want."</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br><br>It's about this overpowering desire and passion that might be able to drawn you under if you let yourself get to caught up in it...<br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417291ra/825165.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This is wrong." I say, panting.<br><br>He grins demonically, nibbling my lip. "All the best things are," he agrees. "Now close your eyes, Gemma, and go with it. Who cares if it's wrong? How does it feel?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407233ra/795174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"One thing is certain. My judgment becomes compromised when it comes to Phillipe, and I have no immediate idea on how to stop myself from wanting to be compromised over and over again."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417291ra/825166.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><br>Just like Phillipe is starting to pull Gemma under, this story will pull <i>you</i> under... It will pull you under in its intensity, its beauty and its many tragical events. It's a story that will keep you on the edge of your seat and that will make you question what's wrong and what's right. Some of the thins that happen in it might seem disturbing, but because of the way it was written, it just seemed <i>right</i>.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Stay or run?" he questions mimicking the thoughts in my had. "Trust me or trust them?"<br><br>"All I'm telling you, Gemma, is that maybe you should heed what the stories have told you. Maybe you should run. Run far away from me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Blind Obsession</i> is enticing, captivating, dark, gritty, emotional, heartbreaking story about three people being bound together by a passion so deep it's bound to pull them under... It's not an easy story to read, some parts of it hurt. It will mess with your head, but in the end it will be worth it. The way it ended, to me, made perfect sense. It might not have been the happiest way to end it, but it ended in a way that did all of the characters justice.<br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417291ra/825167.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br>What made reading this story such a unique experience was not only the flawless and compelling writing style of the author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6451816.Ella_Frank" title="Ella Frank" rel="nofollow noopener">Ella Frank</a> but also the combination of literature, art and music. Listening to the beautiful and well chosen music on <a href="http://blindobsessionbook.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">This Site</a> will make your reading experience even more compelling and complete. It definitely made my reading experience <b>
  <i>unforgettable</i>
</b> and that <i>Blind Obsession</i> is one of the best books I've read this year/ever. <br><br>I would highly advice you to read it and find out for yourself what this captivating story is all about...<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Love looks not with the yes, but with the mind, and, therefore, is winged cupid blind."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>~~~<br><br><br><br><b>5+++ HAUNTINGLY BEAUTIFUL AND BRILLIANT STARS.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10760042032612696200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer636447434" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7682631806070388479">FIVE STARS, without a doubt. I had been putting off reading this book for ages. I love my Romance books but this one was coming across as a little bit darker and I was not sure where the ending was going…. WOW. I loved it. I hated it. It is a beautifully written piece of art. Yes, it is a piece of art….. I won’t say too much about it as I think you are better off just going straight in and reading it without knowing too much about it. I will sum it up in three words, <b>Heartbreakingly, Hauntingly,</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7682631806070388479" style="display:none">FIVE STARS, without a doubt. I had been putting off reading this book for ages. I love my Romance books but this one was coming across as a little bit darker and I was not sure where the ending was going…. WOW. I loved it. I hated it. It is a beautifully written piece of art. Yes, it is a piece of art….. I won’t say too much about it as I think you are better off just going straight in and reading it without knowing too much about it. I will sum it up in three words, <b>Heartbreakingly, Hauntingly, Beautiful…..</b> <br><br>You MUST listen to the music that is mentioned while reading this book.... if the book doesn't move you, the music certainly will.<br><br><b>Le vrais paradis sont les paradis qu’on a perdus…</b><br> <br> <br><img over.”</b><br> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380424654i/846706._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br> <br><br> <br><img         <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/584734511?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr?shelf=scorching-hot">scorching-hot</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer584734511" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14129073827140023641">Five+++++ turturous, heart wrenching stars! Ella Frank, you have destroyed me with this book! <br/><br/><i>
  <b>Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdus</b>
</i><br/> (The true paradises are paradises we have lost.)<br/><br/>Chateau Tibideau<br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/93cb212538ee7b71167cf9e3238bbfdf_zps63685219.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823668.jpg' alt=' photo 93cb212538ee7b71167cf9e3238bbfdf_zps63685219.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Let me start by saying, this book WILL TOP the best of the best for me for years to come (and I have never once said that before). I knew very early on that I was reading something unlike ANY other book I've ever read. The writing is exquisite, the character development superb, the e</span>
  <span id="freeText14129073827140023641" style="display:none">Five+++++ turturous, heart wrenching stars! Ella Frank, you have destroyed me with this book! <br><br><i>
  <b>Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu'on a perdus</b>
</i><br> (The true paradises are paradises we have lost.)<br><br>Chateau Tibideau<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/93cb212538ee7b71167cf9e3238bbfdf_zps63685219.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823668.jpg" alt=" photo 93cb212538ee7b71167cf9e3238bbfdf_zps63685219.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let me start by saying, this book WILL TOP the best of the best for me for years to come (and I have never once said that before). I knew very early on that I was reading something unlike ANY other book I've ever read. The writing is exquisite, the character development superb, the emotions evoked...a menagerie of love, lust, fear, dread, empathy, emotional torture, and in the end, understanding. It was riveting from beginning to end. <br><br>Blind obsession is listed as erotica. That's not quite good enough for me. It's a stand alone in genre in that the eroticism is artistic and so sensual in nature, typical erotic books almost seem like smut compared to it. This is the first in Ella Frank's "erotica" writing and she did a stellar job. Take note, however, this is nothing like her typical romance novels. It's very dark, mysterious and captivates you at the start. I personally felt like the erotica took a back seat to such an awesome storyline. But rest assured, there's a reason it's listed as erotica. Wow!<br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440292.jpg" alt=" photo jordan2_zps58d4d900.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"&gt;<br><br>First and foremost, try to make Internet available while reading this book. Ella has a companion website and it has all the music that corresponds to scenes in the book. That heightened the experience tenfolds. In fact, I've downloaded many of the beautiful music for reading background enjoyment. This is yet another way Ms Frank has added to the whole experience this book provides. It takes a scene and you literally feel as if you are there. <br><br>The story- this is not just a story of two people who meet and fall in love- it's a tale of three. Gemma Harris is a journalist assigned to go to Chateau Tibideau in France to interview Phillip, an infamous artist who's at the center of a dark tale of lust and loss. Philippe is a social recluse since these "events" occurred and hateful stories have made news. She is being sent to get the real story from this mysterious man. It's the job that'll make or break her career. Hopefully she can survive the details of that fateful day by his personal accounts and that of a journal left behind....<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=626e9c45716d2a26ec60a9db2982c392_zps7f505646.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391871799i/8468943._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Like I said, if you're looking for a fluffy love story, look elsewhere. This book is quite dark and, at times, very sad. Philippe is living in his own private hell, in a chateau crumbling to the ground, but he can't leave <i>her</i>......his soul, <i>her</i> soul is here...where she left it....when she left. This life is his punishment but the world needs to know their story, their truth and Gemma was purposefully chosen to bring that story to life. What Gemma doesn't bank on is her feelings that evolve for the man she's interviewing.<br><br>In order to get a true sense of the events that take place, Gemma and Philippe pseudo-recreate what happened.....the story of Philippe and Chantel, the love of his life. His muse..... Chantel was blind, an accomplished violinist, and as different from Gemma as night and day. <br><br><i>
  <b>Love looks not with the eyes but with the mind, and therefore, is winged Cupid painted blind.</b>
</i><br><br>Casting of Philippe- (all taken from blindobsessionbook.com)<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Male%20Eye%20Candy/8517d203dfa3e93a8047ca2b59cc36a6_zps23c4cf3e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823669.jpg" alt=" photo 8517d203dfa3e93a8047ca2b59cc36a6_zps23c4cf3e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gemma-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Women%20for%20reviews/7b502142be2f44f7a233d1ee0af21268_zps7b06ac37.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390700i/752578.jpg" alt=" photo 7b502142be2f44f7a233d1ee0af21268_zps7b06ac37.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Chantel-<br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Women%20for%20reviews/562e7049e7ae3c66791363504e0bee8e_zps5a80bde4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823670.jpg" alt=" photo 562e7049e7ae3c66791363504e0bee8e_zps5a80bde4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>In the recreation of "their story," Philippe paints the Blind Vision Collection of paintings with Gemma as a model. These were originally done with Chantel and are beautifully erotic and are displayed in the Chateau. During these sessions, Gemma interviews Philippe, getting a feeling of how his relationship with his blind muse evolved. As these paintings evolve, the erotic scenes come into play. These scenes as artistically produced as the art before them....sensual and intense. <br><br>The book is a dichotomy of push and pull. Philippe is haunted by his love of Chantel. He's torn between faithfulness to her and a growing desire for Gemma. Gemma, in reading her journal, almost feels the sense of her presence in the chateau. It's not like it's just her and Philippe in the room, it's like she's there.....<br><br><i>
  <b>The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision.</b>
</i><br><br>So if you're up for a read that's dark, gritty, torturous, and NOT happy fluff, this is your book. But I also realize this book is not for everyone. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[If a HEA is a must for you, this book unfortunately will not produce that. I thought I'd need it for a great rating, but the book is so phenomenal, I'm good with it. It wouldn't be the same if she threw in some fluffy ending, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps7fdca565.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823671.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps7fdca565.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> Log onto <b><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.blindobsessionbook.com">www.blindobsessionbook.com</a></b> and listen to the beautifully chosen music as it occurs in the book. You will be amazed how it heightens your experience. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/image_zps37039b9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823672.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps37039b9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Bravo Ella Frank. Allison has a new favorite book evah!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/6c57295831c410ac16bfbc6d3e4f71e1_zpsed2d8c24.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416809i/823673._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6c57295831c410ac16bfbc6d3e4f71e1_zpsed2d8c24.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>The following link in the final chapter in Philippe's POV that Ella posted on 4/24/13. Do not read this until after you've read the book. Huge spoiler alert...... <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/final-impressions-phillipes-pov/">http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/fina...</a><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      Candace

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475308931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5932523447046673481"><br/><br/><b> FIVE EXQUISITE, OBSESSIVE, CRAZY & PASSIONATE STARS </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776392.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>How can I review this amazing book? I don’t know if I will be able to but I will try my best.<br/><br/>Let me say I loved Ella Frank on her Exquisite series but this book… This book is so much more than that, this is one of the best erotic novels I have ever read, period.<br/><br/>I cannot spoil anything for you because I know my Pip, Candace, will spank me and as much as I would love her to do that I just want you all to experience this book without knowing anyt</span>
  <span id="freeText5932523447046673481" style="display:none"><br><br><b> FIVE EXQUISITE, OBSESSIVE, CRAZY &amp; PASSIONATE STARS </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776392.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How can I review this amazing book? I don’t know if I will be able to but I will try my best.<br><br>Let me say I loved Ella Frank on her Exquisite series but this book… This book is so much more than that, this is one of the best erotic novels I have ever read, period.<br><br>I cannot spoil anything for you because I know my Pip, Candace, will spank me and as much as I would love her to do that I just want you all to experience this book without knowing anything about it. I want you to feel how the characters involve you in their story, I want you to feel you are a part of their lives.<br><br>The story commences with Gemma traveling to France to interview Philippe, one of the most famous artists in the world. When she arrives in his chateau she has a difficult task, she needs him to open up and tell her a hard yet beautiful story and that’s when Gemma gets to meet Chantel, a mysterious musician who also is Philippe’s muse.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776393._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Philippe is broken, fucked up, totally lost and Gemma tries to help him as much as she can but I guess you can’t help someone that doesn’t ask for help, can you?<br><br>And he has a HUGE problem, he is OBSESSED with Chantel and let me tell you that’s wrong. In my opinion that was his biggest problem. He is stuck in his past, his happiness is based on another person and oh my god, that’s just terrible.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Obsession: the state of being obsessed with someone or something.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776394.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Philippe needs to learn that the only thing that exist is the present and that was his mistake. He probably needs a conversation with Eckart Tolle, he needs to learn the power of now. Because Philippe, let me tell you that the only real thing is the now.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776395._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I finished this book 24 hours ago and I still don’t know what to say in my review, I know I need to come back and complete this at some point but at this moment I just don’t know what else to say.<br><br>I just loved Ella’s writing style. This book was hot, ok, I am not going to deny this but this is not what captivated me. I was captivated by the original story, by three amazing yet complicated characters and by amazing surroundings.<br><br>As Baba mentioned, we got to read one of the best erotic scenes at 74%, Ella you ROCK and you have probably ruined my future erotic M/F novels…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400528i/776396.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the end… Loved it, big time. I wouldn’t change ANYTHING as the story wouldn’t feel that real. That is all.<br><br>If you have finished this amazing book, go read last chapter in Philippe’s POV. Do NOT read it unless you have finish this book:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/final-impressions-phillipes-pov/">http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/fina...</a><br><br><b> I wanted to add more thoughts/quotes about this book but I really don't want to spoil the story so that's all for now...<br><br></b></span>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/475190062?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475190062" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10800406764053423759"><b>4.5 Obsessed Stars! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/87146792-cecb-4936-b4c3-a8e9d7a75331_zpsb0d8dbbf.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776268.jpg' alt=' photo 87146792-cecb-4936-b4c3-a8e9d7a75331_zpsb0d8dbbf.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>How do you review a book like this? I am at a loss for words. It’s been days since I’ve read this, and I’ve been putting off reviewing it. I don’t know what to say or where to start, but I’ll give it a go. This is a story of obsession. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/2d2640bd-1477-436d-8c51-413567ee657b_zps7562231b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776269.jpg' alt=' photo 2d2640bd-1477-436d-8c51-413567ee657b_zps7562231b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>The domination of one’s thoughts or feelings by a persistent idea, image or desire... </b><br/><br/>Phillipe Tibideau had an obsession. And her name was Chantel Rosenberg. She was his inspiration in all things. Love, life, art, beauty. Phillipe was n</span>
  <span id="freeText10800406764053423759" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Obsessed Stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/87146792-cecb-4936-b4c3-a8e9d7a75331_zpsb0d8dbbf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776268.jpg" alt=" photo 87146792-cecb-4936-b4c3-a8e9d7a75331_zpsb0d8dbbf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>How do you review a book like this? I am at a loss for words. It’s been days since I’ve read this, and I’ve been putting off reviewing it. I don’t know what to say or where to start, but I’ll give it a go. This is a story of obsession. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/2d2640bd-1477-436d-8c51-413567ee657b_zps7562231b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776269.jpg" alt=" photo 2d2640bd-1477-436d-8c51-413567ee657b_zps7562231b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>The domination of one’s thoughts or feelings by a persistent idea, image or desire... </b><br><br>Phillipe Tibideau had an obsession. And her name was Chantel Rosenberg. She was his inspiration in all things. Love, life, art, beauty. Phillipe was never happier than when he was with Chantel. But now she is gone and everything is different. Phillipe is a haunted man. He is a broken man. He is still living in the past. <br><br><b>Who is Phillipe Tibideau? </b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a6881a8e-9e00-4113-a9d8-b2f8a7e6fa15_zps37842124.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776270.jpg" alt=" photo a6881a8e-9e00-4113-a9d8-b2f8a7e6fa15_zps37842124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There was a tragic accident, and Phillipe has completely kept to himself at Chateau Tibideau ever since. Now, he is ready to open up, to tell his side of the story. <br><br>Enter journalist Gemma Harris-<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/f5cdc673-4d65-402f-a48c-22cdcde66180_zps3a7080c0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776271.jpg" alt=" photo f5cdc673-4d65-402f-a48c-22cdcde66180_zps3a7080c0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gemma is the opposite of Chantel in the looks department, but somehow, Phillipe finds him self drawn to her. Gemma is drawn to Phillipe, but after reading Chantel’s thoughts, she finds herself equally drawn to her. <br><b>
  <blockquote>He touches me with every look he gives me, and she touches me with every word she tells me.</blockquote>
</b><br>Gemma is living with Phillipe, interviewing him, while reading Chantel’s journal at the same time. She feels a connection to the both of them. Their love story is unconventional, yet beautiful. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/a9d57779-6127-43d8-b7bd-1a01214c0bfe_zps0b8a5f21.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776272.jpg" alt=" photo a9d57779-6127-43d8-b7bd-1a01214c0bfe_zps0b8a5f21.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Phillipe is still very much in love with Chantel. He still feels her presence through the music and his paintings. He is in a dark haze. Gemma slowly starts to unravel him, and it freaks him out. He decides to paint Gemma, in the same poses that he painted Chantel <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but all he ever truly sees is Chantel. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Phillipe and Gemma’s relationship was... complicated.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3ab7d3b7-030a-4b2a-895f-4b7750551a4a_zps6132e935.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776273._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 3ab7d3b7-030a-4b2a-895f-4b7750551a4a_zps6132e935.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Phillipe and Gemma together were sensual and sexy, but <i>she</i> was always with them...<br><b>
  <blockquote>When did this story morph? When did it change from a tale of two to a tragedy of three?</blockquote>
</b><br>After finishing this book, I just sat there, thinking for an hour. I had so much going through my head. I don’t even know how I feel about the ending. This book will leave you with a serious book hangover. I know this isn't really a 'full' review, but its the best I can do right now. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3c91f19b-2df9-4fe0-af1b-db0e4e809e55_zpsae15bec8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400510i/776274.jpg" alt=" photo 3c91f19b-2df9-4fe0-af1b-db0e4e809e55_zpsae15bec8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I love you. That is the beginning, that is the end. That is everything.” </blockquote>
</b><br>This story was profound. I was captivated by it the moment I picked it up. It was like no other book I have ever read. It was a bit of a mind fuck, but that just made it that much better. I enjoyed Exquisite and Entice by Ella Frank, but this book was in a whole different league! The writing was amazing. This book is intense, sexy, dark, passionate, beautiful and haunting. The sex scenes were erotic and tasteful. I fell in love with the three characters in this, and I will not be forgetting this one anytime soon!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="10800406764053423759" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer588621649" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12291699194899063208"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417384ra/825469.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_llxkiarOgp1qii6tmo1_500_zps6dd782dc.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>So many great reviews have been written about this great book and I don’t think I have enough words to write down that would do justice to this incredible story, so I am going to give some of my feelings and thoughts about Blind Obsession.<br/><blockquote><b>Breathtakingly Beautiful and Unforgettable<br/>Overwhelmingly Dark and Intense<br/>Painful and Haunting<br/>Sensual and Erotic<br/>Devastatingly Emotional<br/>Awe-inspiring and Evocative<br/>Powerful and Consuming</b></blockquote>This is one of those extraordinary books that consumed me and will haunt me fo</span>
  <span id="freeText12291699194899063208" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417384ra/825469.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_llxkiarOgp1qii6tmo1_500_zps6dd782dc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So many great reviews have been written about this great book and I don’t think I have enough words to write down that would do justice to this incredible story, so I am going to give some of my feelings and thoughts about Blind Obsession.<br><blockquote><b>Breathtakingly Beautiful and Unforgettable<br>Overwhelmingly Dark and Intense<br>Painful and Haunting<br>Sensual and Erotic<br>Devastatingly Emotional<br>Awe-inspiring and Evocative<br>Powerful and Consuming</b></blockquote>This is one of those extraordinary books that consumed me and will haunt me for a long time. I found myself lost in this compelling story that evoked so many emotions from me, which pulled me right in and into the world and inside the heads of Phillipe, Gemma &amp; Chantel.<br><br>Seeing it from the 3 different POV’s was it made it such a powerful story. Seeing their journey through their eyes. Using Chantel’s diary was a fantastic and innovative way in showing how strong her influence was in the relationship between Phillipe &amp; Gemma. What an “original” take on a menage story!!!! <br><br>And the experience of listening to the music that Chantel played and the pictures of Phillipe’s paintings totally blew me away. A sensory overdrive trip – sight and sound…an absolutely and incredible and unique way to enhance a reading experience. Truly Amazing.<br><br>Meditation by Jules Massenet –sad and haunting. Winter from Four Seasons by Vivaldi – I have listened to this piece of music before but never have I been so affected by it as I was reading this book. Lux Aternea by Clive Mansell….beautiful, just beautiful.Check out the author’s site <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://blindobsessionbook.com">http://blindobsessionbook.com</a> that has links to the music and paintings she uses in the book.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417384i/825470.jpg" alt=" photo diva_zps7bd90b57.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Ah…violins….I will forever be reminded of Chantel…<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>All along I had such a strong belief that Gemma would be the right person to get through Phillipe’s pain and heartache and that in some way he would be able to rise from the darkness and emptiness in his life in since Chantel’s sad and tragic death. Even in the last pages I still had hope…<span>[image error]</span><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417384ra/825471.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mocb95gCB11rkbqbko1_500_zpsc468eb5c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>And despite all my guessing and hoping, I was still stunned by the unpredictable ending. <br><br><b><blockquote>Ella Frank said “My goal is to immerse you in this book by giving you the opportunity to view the images and hear the music that is discussed.”</blockquote></b><br>You did immerse me in this beautiful story and I just want to say <b>‘Thank You”.</b><br><br>Read this book. No other story will rip your heart to pieces like this one did to me. You will read it in one “go”…you will be held spellbound until the last page. And you will shed a tear or two or three, like I did!!!! <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417384i/825472.jpg" alt=" photo images3_zpsdce410b2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And you won’t be able to put it down…no matter what!!!<br><blockquote><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417384ra/825473.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lrs97jJHzh1r3v6f2o1_400_zpsd14bc8ab.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <a title="KatLynne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KatLynne" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne">KatLynne</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer518561661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16863745685350776473"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><b> Riveting! Darkly Erotic! Intense! Passionate!</b><br/><br/><b>Note</b> - There are only pictures under each <b>spoiler tag</b> until the very end.:) <br/><br/><b>Blind Obsession</b> is Ella Frank’s first venture into Erotic Fiction and she gives a stellar performance. This isn’t a book that you merely read; instead, it's one to be <b>EXPERIENCED</b> in all its artistic flavor. Every emotion will be engaged in this hauntingly beautiful masterpiece. <br/><br/>It all began at Chateau Tibideau, where two souls became one. Here you will find the kind </span>
  <span id="freeText16863745685350776473" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><br><b> Riveting! Darkly Erotic! Intense! Passionate!</b><br><br><b>Note</b> - There are only pictures under each <b>spoiler tag</b> until the very end.:) <br><br><b>Blind Obsession</b> is Ella Frank’s first venture into Erotic Fiction and she gives a stellar performance. This isn’t a book that you merely read; instead, it's one to be <b>EXPERIENCED</b> in all its artistic flavor. Every emotion will be engaged in this hauntingly beautiful masterpiece. <br><br>It all began at Chateau Tibideau, where two souls became one. Here you will find the kind of love only experienced once in a lifetime....<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/MBrbRs1364609272_zps5210c20b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440288._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MBrbRs1364609272_zps5210c20b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>A place where breathtakingly beautiful melodies haunt every aspect of the chateau. It's as if the music is a living, breathing entity and adds a melancholic feel.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/Woman-playing-the-violin-007_zps68a4b963.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440289.jpg" alt=" photo Woman-playing-the-violin-007_zps68a4b963.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>A place consumed by passion; desire; cravings.<br><b> “This was what it felt like to want.”</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/intense_zps0e7aa719.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440290.jpg" alt=" photo intense_zps0e7aa719.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>... “He wanted to create something that moved people – a piece so fucking brilliant that people would cry when they looked at it. He wanted to alter their emotions and to touch their soul.”</b><br><br>A place where his vision came to fruition and his creations touched the world. And within all his glorious talent, he discovered that all he <i>really</i> wanted or needed was to touch <b>her.</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/chantel-bw_zps90c5659e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440291._SY540_.jpg" alt="Chantel photo chantel-bw_zps90c5659e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There was a time when he had it all. Now, he's haunted by a past that has left him broken; a past that refuses to release him and one that he can't let go. <br><br>The world thinks he's a monster. Phillipe has decided it's time to tell his side of the story even knowing he will be ripped apart again in unimaginable pain. He invites reporter Gemma Harris into his home. She’s intrigued and eagerly accepts his offer. Little did she know her life would soon be forever changed...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Couples/jordan2_zps58d4d900.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440292.jpg" alt=" photo jordan2_zps58d4d900.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>"Right now you're mine, just like <i>she</i> was mine. I'm going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can't forget."</b><br><br>The setting is beautiful and Chantel's presence is everywhere. The entire chateau is surrounded by the melancholy music she once played. The paintings not only portray her beauty but the remarkable talent of Phillipe. As Gemma is consumed by her own hunger for Phillipe, she wonders if she is being compared to <i>her.</i> As the story progresses and she discovers Chantel, her feelings dramatically change. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/PhillipeandGemma_zps72903448.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440293._SX540_.jpg" alt="Phillipe and Gemma Dancing photo PhillipeandGemma_zps72903448.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <br>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Phillipe Tibideau</b> oozes sexiness. Wickedly delicious and tremendously talented, he's irresistible. Not only is he one of the most sexiest heroes I've read, he's also one of the most tortured. He's unforgettable. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <a href="http://s1256.photobucket.com/user/KatLynne5/media/Blind%20Obsession/Matthias-Streitwieser-5_zpsf8e18eac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783012i/440294._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Matthias-Streitwieser-5_zpsf8e18eac.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This story is surrounded by mystery, plunging the reader into the shadows and darkness of this journey. The best way for Gemma to know Chantel is through her journals. Through these pages the reader is swept away into one of the most beautiful, erotic, touching yet tragic love stories I've read. <br><br>And where does Gemma fit into all this? How does she compete with a once in a lifetime love? What happens when the other half of you is no longer available?<br><br>The writing is superb and you’ll become completely immersed as you experience the feelings of each character. Ella Frank’s talent easily manipulates your emotions, leaving you raw, breathless and shattered at times. The interactive quality is brilliantly done adding such depth to an already well crafted tale. <br><br>This is not a light and fluffy read. It's an emotionally intense highly Erotic tale completely different from Ms. Frank's Contemporaries. The passion is palpable; the emotion is riveting; and the allure is not to be denied.<br> <br><b>This is NOT a picture but an actual spoiler!!</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The ending is bittersweet and perfect. After pondering the conclusion I realized it could be no other way. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><b>Have you ever had a moment of passion that was so deep and so f&amp;cking perfect that you know you will never have it again?".....</b><br><br><b>-- Prepare to be captivated!</b><br><br><i>ARC courtesy of Ella Frank in exchange for an honest review. Thank you Ella. It was such a pleasure!</i><br><br><b>Incredible trailer.....</b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WfCzNfaW7CU&amp;feature=youtu.be">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=WfCzNf...</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16863745685350776473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

As a journalist, she needed a piece that would propel her career trajectory. That opportunity took her to Bordeaux, France and into the lives of music maven Chantel Rosenberg and reclusive artist Phillipe Tibideau, thus embarking into a journey of unraveling the truth that would change each of their lives.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499077857i/23188499.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“Right now, you’re mine, just like she was mine. I’m goin</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11595901905688747646" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Erotica <br><b>Type: </b>Standalone <br><b>POV: </b>Shifting – Multiple <br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498877613i/23169427.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521771750i/25258849._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gemma Harris had an opportunity she had been waiting all her life. That opportunity took her to Bordeaux, France and into the lives of music maven Chantel Rosenberg and reclusive artist Phillipe Tibideau, thus embarking into a journey of unraveling the truth that would change each of their lives.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1499077857i/23188499.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

</blockquote><br><br>I had this book on my TBR for a long time. I'm so glad to finally get to read it because I truly enjoyed the story. This book offered something different with the dynamics between the characters. Each of them had their own appeal and added dimension to the book.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1521771750i/25258850._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book had a lot of scorching sexy scenes. But instead of it being a mindless distraction, it added intensity to the angsty story. I also love the dark, eerie feel of the story. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>If she wants to go down this rabbit hole with him, then she better be prepared for what she will find.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Blind Obsession is a haunting tale of an all-consuming love. It would appeal to fans of erotica with element of mystery and romance.<br><br><br><br><br><b>For more reviews/reveals/giveaways visit:</b><br><a href="http://warhawkevault.wordpress.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_475251585" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/475251585" />
    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/475251585?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=mind-f-k">mind-f-k</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=wrecked">wrecked</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=2013-faves">2013-faves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475251585" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10954983224345585578"><b>5+++++ stars!</b><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776321.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision”</blockquote>
</b> <br/>In the special introduction of this novel Ella Frank states <i>“My goal is to immerse you in this book by giving you the opportunity to view the images and hear the music that is discussed.”</i> And <i>“At its core, this novel is about the amazing power of the senses that we, as humans, possess. Sight and sound are the two I hope to bring to you.”</i><br/><br/>OMG… did she ever bring them to me! I am sitting at my computer with e</span>
  <span id="freeText10954983224345585578" style="display:none"><b>5+++++ stars!</b><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400519ra/776321.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><b>
  <blockquote>“The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision”</blockquote>
</b> <br>In the special introduction of this novel Ella Frank states <i>“My goal is to immerse you in this book by giving you the opportunity to view the images and hear the music that is discussed.”</i> And <i>“At its core, this novel is about the amazing power of the senses that we, as humans, possess. Sight and sound are the two I hope to bring to you.”</i><br><br>OMG… did she ever bring them to me! I am sitting at my computer with earbuds in and listening to <i>Air by Johann Sebastian Bach</i> and hours after I finished reading this book, I still have a lump in my throat. I can’t remember the last time a book grabbed me and totally immersed me in it. I felt the love, the lust, the music, the art, the wine country of France and I fell in love with a dead blind women and her Stradivarius violin named, ‘Diva’<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400519i/776322.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br> Journalist Gemma Harris arrives at Chateau Tibideau in France to interview the infamous artist, Phillipe Tibideau a <i>“man so private and so isolated from the outside world that no one has seen or heard from him in months, ever since he was hounded relentlessly about his involvement in the tragic events that had unfolded here”</i> A story that will either make or break her career.<br><br>This story of a lifetime for Gemma’s profession turns into a life-changing story for her. Through the interview sessions with Phillipe and the journal entries of Chantel; Gemma is caught up in a web of intrigue, salvation, pain and intense love of two people. <br><br>In order to learn the story of what happened to Chantel, Phillipe has Gemma recreate the poses of Chantel’s collection: The Blind Vision Collection.<br>These sessions turn into some of the most captivating erotica I have ever read. No words can describe what I felt while reading (experiencing) this…. <b>intensity</b>… . I was on fire with rapid heart beats; hanging on every descriptive detail. It was a savory-sensational-sensual-sensory overload.<br><br>While the story unfolds, Gemma finds herself in a predicament of loving a very tortured gorgeous man and his once in a lifetime love of a women he can’t let go of.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400519i/776323._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Trust me, I’m not what you want, Gemma. I’m not what you need,” he whispers, stressing his last word. “Don’t waste your time loving me.”But love? Where does she get the absurd notion that I’m capable of loving anything anymore? I’m not even capable of loving myself, let alone someone else."</b>
</blockquote> <br><br>Even though Chantel is gone from this earth she is everywhere and Phillipe will not have it any other way even while he is with Gemma he still sees Chantel, or does he?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“You’ve fucking destroyed me. First, she did, and now, you are.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373247ra/726782.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story gets harder for Gemma to write, she is too caught up in her feelings for Phillipe as well as Chantel: <br><br><b>"When did this story morph? When did it change from a tale of two to a tragedy of three?"</b><br><br>And what a story this is. It will mess with your mind, heart and soul. This book rocked my world and I know I will be reading it again because it is so hauntingly beautiful. <br><br>It is very hard to write a review that comes close to expressing what I thought about this book without giving more detail and I don't want to tell any more of the story. I want you, the reader to fully experience this amazing book.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"For the lady we never let go of. Blind Obsession You are both mine."</blockquote>
</b> <br><br> <br>*<i>Thank you, Ella Frank for providing a copy for an honest and heartfelt review. As I told you before, I truly loved this book.</i> <b>XOXO</b><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10954983224345585578" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
