<span id="freeTextContainer5109214926277235556"><b> This review may or may not make sense, due to my lack of being able to do that putting-together-words thing. So bear with me, okay?</b><br/><br/>When I finished this book last night, I had no <i> idea </i> how I was going to pull off a review for it. <br/><br/>My thoughts were scattered.<br/>My eyelashes were tangled with tears.<br/>And my heart seemed to dancing to the fastest song it knew.<br/><br/>It’s like Ella Frank only writes with the sexiest, most provocative letters of the alphabet.<br/>She writes this story with those letters, creating sen</span>
  <span id="freeText5109214926277235556" style="display:none"><b> This review may or may not make sense, due to my lack of being able to do that putting-together-words thing. So bear with me, okay?</b><br><br>When I finished this book last night, I had no <i> idea </i> how I was going to pull off a review for it. <br><br>My thoughts were scattered.<br>My eyelashes were tangled with tears.<br>And my heart seemed to dancing to the fastest song it knew.<br><br>It’s like Ella Frank only writes with the sexiest, most provocative letters of the alphabet.<br>She writes this story with those letters, creating sensual on top of erotic on top of beautiful… with a livewire of something dark beneath it.<br><br>  <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_md5fxqjrvP1r36hklo1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><u>
  <i> Phillipe </i>
</u><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/DAVID_GANDY_ELLE_MAN_CHINA_AUGUST_2012_LIONEL_GUYOU-4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>A man whose heart is tortured by a ghost in his lungs.<br><br>He’s an artist.<br>He’s a recluse.<br>He’s sex.<br>He’s beautiful.<br>And he’s <i>very</i> talented with everything that has to do with a paintbrush.<br><br>♦ He is also in love/infatuated with/haunted by a woman who no longer exists. ♦<br><br><u>
  <i> Chantel </i>
</u><br><br>The violinist who fell in love with Phillipe as powerfully as he fell in love with her.<br><br>They fell in love in a way that the world, who watched them, called unhealthy/obsessive/perverse.<br><br>And the world wanted to know Chantel. They wanted to know the woman in the paintings that became Phillipe’s most famous art collection.<br><br>But something happens – something tragic – to Chantel.<br><br>Now Phillipe is haunted by this woman and can’t let go. Because he loves her in a way that <i>can’t</i> let her go.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_mea7wwJuF61qb7o0vo1_500.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>Even when he meets a journalist who comes into his life with a question that the entire world wants to know.<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i> What happened to Chantel Rosenberg? </i>
</b> ♦<br><br><u>
  <i> Gemma </i>
</u><br><br>The journalist.<br>The journalist who has a million questions about one man’s secret.<br>The journalist who becomes infatuated with that one man’s secret.<br><br>As Gemma stays a Phillipe’s chateau, she becomes involved. <br><br>With both the secret at hand, and the man telling the secret, creating one <i>hell</i> of a love triangle. <br><br><i>
  <b> If there was obsession here – a dominant persistent desire – then it was the desire to lose ourselves in one another. The only problem is that one person is now lost, and the other is trapped. </b>
</i><br><br>Phillipe gives Chantel’s journal to Gemma. And as Gemma reads it, she <i>too</i> falls in love with mysterious Chantel.<br><br>But Gemma also falls in love with Phillipe.<br><br>And as the story unfolds, she finds herself competing with Chantel for Phillipe’s heart in a game that doesn’t seem to have any rules.<br><br>But regardless of who wins… the question always remains:<br><br>♦ <b>
  <i> What happened to Chantel Rosenberg? </i>
</b> ♦<br><br> <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/ashleeporte/media/tumblr_m4qtd5INsA1r2fr72o1_500.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_566228104" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/566228104" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/566228104?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=female-pov">female-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=fav-book-boyfriend">fav-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=arc-gifted">arc-gifted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=meli-s-top-favourites">meli-s-top-favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=mind-f-ck">mind-f-ck</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer566228104" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17854329855922869400"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816192._SX540_.jpg' width='150' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>*** 5 Hauntingly Beautiful Tragic Stars ***<br/>Spoiler Free</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816193._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I think for you to understand this story, you must first become a part of it."</i>
</b><br/><br/>This is not your ordinary Erotic novel, this was an intensely heartbreaking story. I was captivated by the mystery that surrounded Chateau Tibideau from the very beginning. I could not put this down.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Love looks not with the eyes but with the mind, and, therefore, is winged cupid painted blind."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Phillipe Tibideau thinks it's time for the real story to be tol</span>
  <span id="freeText17854329855922869400" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816192._SX540_.jpg" width="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>*** 5 Hauntingly Beautiful Tragic Stars ***<br>Spoiler Free</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816193._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"I think for you to understand this story, you must first become a part of it."</i>
</b><br><br>This is not your ordinary Erotic novel, this was an intensely heartbreaking story. I was captivated by the mystery that surrounded Chateau Tibideau from the very beginning. I could not put this down.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Love looks not with the eyes but with the mind, and, therefore, is winged cupid painted blind."</i>
</b><br><br>Phillipe Tibideau thinks it's time for the real story to be told, the story about <i>her</i>, Chantel Rosenberg. He invites journalist, Gemma Harris, to stay several months in his Chateau, so she can write about how things <i>really</i> occured. Gemma can't believe she is staying at Chateau Tibideau for a few months, regardless to the warnings she had received about Phillipe. Why is this once famous artist, that is now living in seclusion, being referred to as a 'Beautiful Monster'. She is determined to find out the truth, and to see if all the assumptions made in the media about him, have any validity to them. Gemma, is given Chantel's journal, so she can get inside her head during the time Chantel had a relationship with Phillipe. Gemma never knew, she would never be the same.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816194._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Phillipe was so intense, that he constantly had my heart racing. There was just this mysterious sexiness to him but also a haunting sadness that would enthrall you and not let go. No matter how scary at times he behaved, a part of you still wanted to stay to discover the real man beneath that broken exterior, the man that was written in that journal. He had me in a constant arousal throughout the book and his seduction wasn't just affecting Gemma, but me as well. I could actually <i>feel</i> the touches, the soft breaths, and the smooth sound of his voice caress my skin. The sex scenes were <i>Really</i> HOT, I am talking high steam here. You will really love it!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Beauty." There's a pregnant pause before he repeats himself louder. "Beauty inspired me."<br>"Beauty of the world?"<br>"No, beauty of a woman. One woman."</i>
</b><br><br>I have never felt a connection so strong to a character as I felt with Gemma. I felt and thought everything she was feeling and thinking. It was almost as if we were one and the same. It was like I was having my own taste of what Gemma was going through when reading Chantel's journal. The writing was just truly brilliant. I became addicted to Phillipe and Chantel's love story but also how Gemma seemed to intertwine with them and become obsessed with Chantel. Throughout the story, it felt as though Chantel was never gone, you could always feel her presence in some way.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816195._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book was written in such a way, that you could see everything that was happening as if you were watching a movie reel being played inside your head. Except that you feel as though you are a part of it, not just spectating it. I loved the idea of incorporating those interactions, it brought everything to life and really helped me have an engaging reading experience. I was using the interactions while reading and my senses were completely titillated. I found myself being swept away by the beautiful music and paintings. I give big props to Ella Frank for including this great idea into her book.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I want you to play for me"<br>"What would you like me to play?"<br>"...how about something that will haunt me?"<br>"That I can do"</i>
</b><br><br>This is definitely a story that will stick with me for a very long time. I have never felt such a raw heartache from reading a book. Ella Frank struck gold when writing this fantastic book. I definitely recommend you experience this beautiful and intense tragic story for yourself. So make sure to grab a copy on <b>April 9th</b>!! Thank you to Ella Frank for allowing me to read such an AMAZING book!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"The true paradises are paradises we have lost."</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>Phillipe<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396390i/764042._SY540_.jpg" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gemma<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816196._SX540_.jpg" width="340" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Chantel</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414139i/816197.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>***Arc provided by author, Ella Frank, in exchange for an honest review.***</b><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17854329855922869400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593242030?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>

<span id="freeTextContainer15230100676679989146"><b>5 Amazingly Beautiful and Obsessive Stars<br/><br/><i>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu’on a perdus."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827468.jpg' width='400' height='280' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sometimes we all start to wonder how it feels to see with a touch, hear with a glance, entice with a smile and enthrall with a thought. How to use all our senses, to heighten the passion, to open the soul and experience the magnificence that hides in each one of us. To find the one thing that makes us unique, because <i>Beauty is in the eye of the Beholder</i> but people don't always see with their eyes.... And</span>
  <span id="freeText15230100676679989146" style="display:none"><b>5 Amazingly Beautiful and Obsessive Stars<br><br><i>"Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu’on a perdus."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827468.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sometimes we all start to wonder how it feels to see with a touch, hear with a glance, entice with a smile and enthrall with a thought. How to use all our senses, to heighten the passion, to open the soul and experience the magnificence that hides in each one of us. To find the one thing that makes us unique, because <i>Beauty is in the eye of the Beholder</i> but people don't always see with their eyes.... And we do tend to forget, that there is always so much more to it.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Everything has beauty, but not everyone sees it."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/547637.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Phillipe Tibideau</b> artist of an acclaimed Series of paintings "Blind Vision", dabbed as <i>
  <b>“an alluring mixture of dark eroticism enhanced now by its devastatingly haunting sadness”</b>
</i>, has secluded himself in his home in the French countryside. After a devastating event that made him a monster in the public eye, he has withdrawn, stopped painting and producing wine and refusing to talk to anyone. Alluring, passionate, almost manic, obsessed, beautiful and talented he will draw you into his web and his story will entice and awaken forgotten and deliciously forbidden passions.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827469.jpg" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>He decides to grant entrance to one reporter and share his side of the story. In his own time and in his own way, <b>Gemma Harris</b> the young reporter will be given the chance to find out his truth and learn a bit about herself along the way. <br><br><i>
  <b>"I'd heard about people falling in love, and I'd heard about lust. What I had never heard of was this all-consuming need to be inside another human being. I felt this desperate compulsion to become one with him. This was desire. This was to crave. This was what it felt like to want."</b>
</i><br><br>Falling under the spell of the irresistible, obsessed artist...<br><br><i>
  <b>“Obsession, as defined by the dictionary, means the domination of one’s thoughts or feelings by a persistent idea, image, or desire.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417069ra/824515.gif" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Starting to unravel the heartbreaking story will "introduce" her to <b>Chantel Rosenberg</b> the third part of this alluring and unique love triangle. The blind, talented, stunning woman, the muse to Phillipe's talent...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827470._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>These 3 people will lay their souls bare, strip away any inhibitions and free their hearts to love and passion. Chantel's diary will be the driving force behind Gemma and Phillipe, guiding them to awaken their senses and redefine themselves through each other. Meanwhile her haunting presence will enrapture and enthrall, making her the narrator and catalyst in this story. Because what we romance readers, sometimes forget, because we are used to superficial emotions, is that:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827471.jpg" width="400" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6451816.Ella_Frank" title="Ella Frank" rel="nofollow noopener">Ella Frank</a> presents us with an unforgettable read. She expertly weaves music, art, love and people and with a fluent and erotic writing style, draws you right in and makes you part of this book. You live in the Chateau, you pose for Phillipe, you see with your painted hands like Chantel and you are aroused along with Gemma by a ghost and her maker or was it undo-er? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827472.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Highly Recommended, terrific, amazing, irresistible, sexy, arousing, <b>ΚΑΤΑΠΛΗΚΤΙΚΟ</b>, haunting, lyrical, obsessive and eye opening in a way that only a blind man can understand. Souls also have eyes; using only the obvious ones have weakened them... Love needs them all!<br><br><i><b>"I love you. That is the beginning and that is the end. That is everything."</b></i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418051i/827473._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></b></span>

<div id="review_590979884" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/590979884" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/590979884?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=erotica-romantica-read">erotica-romantica-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=copy-from-author-read">copy-from-author-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer590979884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17630689983397340062">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><br/>3.5 Stars<br/><br/>GENRE: Erotica<br/>HEAT LEVEL: Very Hot<br/>ANGST LEVEL: *Extreme*<br/><br/><br/>Reader Beware........<br/><br/>-The Story-<br/>Phillipe Tibideau is a man haunted by and obsessed with memories of Chantel Rosenberg. A passionate and gifted musician and a world-renowned artist, their connection to one another ran deep and changed both of their lives. All Phillipe wants now is to be left alone, to live his life in seclusion. However, journalist Gemma Harris has other plans. She is seeking t</span>
  <span id="freeText17630689983397340062" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><br />3.5 Stars<br /><br />GENRE: Erotica<br />HEAT LEVEL: Very Hot<br />ANGST LEVEL: *Extreme*<br /><br /><br />Reader Beware........<br /><br />-The Story-<br />Phillipe Tibideau is a man haunted by and obsessed with memories of Chantel Rosenberg. A passionate and gifted musician and a world-renowned artist, their connection to one another ran deep and changed both of their lives. All Phillipe wants now is to be left alone, to live his life in seclusion. However, journalist Gemma Harris has other plans. She is seeking the truth. She has questions, and those questions must be posed directly to Phillipe. Traveling to France and Chateau Tibideau, Gemma has no idea the desire, the answers, the darkness which is in store for her.<br /><br />-My Thoughts-<br />I want to be clear. Personally, I feel Ella Frank has a true gift in her ability to craft and shape a story. Her 'voice' is mature and seasoned. When I read one of her books, there is no indication that she is a relatively new author. That said, BLIND OBSESSION, as you've by now heard, is VERY different from her previous books. Her talent and writing ability may have actually reached a new level while writing about Phillipe, Chantel and Gemma. The story itself is masterfully conceived and told. The included links are brilliant and set the scene perfectly. BUT, going into this story without knowing anything, I have to be honest with you and admit to a very real disappointment with several key aspects of BLIND OBSESSION.<br /><br />First, the unrelenting melancholia of this story was too much for me. There was *not one moment* of light in this long, dark tunnel. I enjoy dark books. I love dark and tortured heroes. Up until BLIND OBSESSION, I would have told you, the darker the better. Not any longer. Phillipe Tibideau is, apparently, where I draw my line. As is this story. It was utterly oppressive in its sadness and grief. <br /><br />Discussing what I'm about to will likely make me unpopular in some circles, but I have a strong opinion about this, and I can't simply ignore it. The second aspect I had a very real problem with was the ending. To put it plainly, I felt *thoroughly* cheated. There is no standard, romance-novel happily-ever-after ending here. There isn't even a happy-for-now. There's *nothing*, and readers should know this and have the choice to proceed or not. I traveled this torturously, depressingly, beautiful journey with these characters only to have it end LIKE THAT??!! While I respect the author's need to write her truth, I had become so fully invested in these characters, in this story, that my upset was HUGE, very real and very legitimate!<br /><br />It's now been several days since I finished reading Ella Frank's latest book, and I can honestly tell you that I've still not come to terms with my feelings. I thoughts, perhaps, letting the book settle for several days would change how I felt. But, that isn't the case. Obviously it's a personal preference as the majority of readers are giving BLIND OBSESSION rave reviews.<br /><br />Ella Frank's talent and ability are certainly not in question, and I look forward to future books from this author. I'll end as I began and say: Reader Beware.........<br /><br /><br />**Copy provided by the author in exchange for an honest review**</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/589225449?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fathima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fathima" href="/user/show/5799807-fathima">Fathima</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer589225449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10767291244411773115"><b>
  <i>“Right now, you’re mine, just like she was mine. I’m going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can’t forget.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/BlindObsession_zpsdfa3fd9f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825774._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo BlindObsession_zpsdfa3fd9f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/><b>5 Blindly-obsessed-and-deeply-infatuated stars !!!</b><br/><br/><b> STUNNED !!!<br/><br/>AMAZED !!! <br/><br/>EXHILARATED !!!! <br/><br/>BUT MOST OF ALL , ABSOLUTYELY SPEECHLESS !! </b> <br/><br/>How do you decide that loving something/someone is too much ?? Or more like , how do you decide how much is too much ?? I think , the answer is pretty clear .. Too much is when you've reached a point of obsession , a point of no return</span>
  <span id="freeText10767291244411773115" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Right now, you’re mine, just like she was mine. I’m going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can’t forget.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/BlindObsession_zpsdfa3fd9f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825774._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo BlindObsession_zpsdfa3fd9f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>5 Blindly-obsessed-and-deeply-infatuated stars !!!</b><br><br><b> STUNNED !!!<br><br>AMAZED !!! <br><br>EXHILARATED !!!! <br><br>BUT MOST OF ALL , ABSOLUTYELY SPEECHLESS !! </b> <br><br>How do you decide that loving something/someone is too much ?? Or more like , how do you decide how much is too much ?? I think , the answer is pretty clear .. Too much is when you've reached a point of obsession , a point of no return .. A point where loving someone seems to be the only thing that is keeping you alive ... A point where you believe that you've been possessed by that person ....<br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/obsession1_zpsfe746ca8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825775.jpg" alt=" photo obsession1_zpsfe746ca8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>When was the last time you read a book and had a experience so surreal , that you managed to lose a part of you somewhere between those pages .. An experience so damn heart breaking that you started seeing things in shades of , not black or white , but grey . An experience so hypnotic , that the lines between imagination and reality blurred so easily that you had to keep asking yourself , ' WHAT THE HECK AM I READING ?!!! ' An experience that is bound to pull you deep and drown you in it ... <br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/dreesedinred_zps36d52634.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825776._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo dreesedinred_zps36d52634.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ella Frank's Blind Obsession is one such book , that leaves you mesmerized .. That leaves you breathless , restless and urges you to ask yourself .. ' WHATS NEXT ?!! ' <br><br>Honestly , I was really excited to read this .. The conceptualization , the book trailer , the idea , the book cover , everything about this had me waiting , keeping me on my toes , anticipating it ... And now that I have read it , and that it has left me completely numb &amp; dumb and gave me a sleepless night , it's safe to say that Blind Obsession had made it to my list of absolute fav and a must-read of 2013 !!! <br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/fab_zpscd3a1d92.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417470ra/825777.gif" alt=" photo fab_zpscd3a1d92.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <u> THE STORY : </u>
</b> <br> <br>Gemma Harris is a journalist invited to Chateau Tibideau , home to the man titled as a beautiful monster .. She is to interview him on a tragedy that changed him and his perception of the world . A tragedy so dauntingly bad , it killed the passionate man in him , leaving him a hollowed shell of a man Phillipe Tibideau used to be .. A tragedy that involved the <s>love</s> passion of his life , Chantel Rosenberg . <br><br><b>
  <u> THE CHARACTERS : </u>
</b> <br><br><b>Gemma Harris : </b> A journalist by profession , she comes to the Chateau in hopes of finding out everything about the man who supposedly tainted an angel and made her cry . Gemma is a professional , but meeting Phillipe changes a lot in her .. Her involvement with Chantel and Phillipe's life turns her life into a roller coaster ride , where she is constantly fighting the high's and lows ...<br><br><b> Chantel Rosenberg : </b> The character mostly represented as <i> She </i> or <i> her </i> was the woman who had set Phillipe's artistic world in motion . She was his inspiration , his <i> beauty </i> .. and ultimately , his fall ...<br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/beauty_zpsd590a618.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825778.jpg" alt=" photo beauty_zpsd590a618.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re going to destroy me,” he admitted with a sigh.</i>
</b><br><br>She also is a famous musician .. Her passion ... Her diva ...<br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/stradivarius_zps706e1b1f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825779._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo stradivarius_zps706e1b1f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b> Phillipe Tibideau : </b> The man who made the angel weep .. The man took something pure and sacred and turned into a object of sin .. A man with two sides . One , seen through Chantel's journal - sweet , loving , possessive , passionate and sinfully sexy . And the one seen through Gemma's eyes , still sinfully sexy , but now moody , bossy , confused , guilt ridden , full of hatred for the world , with a bad temper and somewhat sinister ! <br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/seduction_zpsc8ca06c9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825780.jpg" alt=" photo seduction_zpsc8ca06c9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>
  <u> MY THOUGHTS : </u>
</b> <br><br>You already know what my last reaction to this book was , so lets just leave it to that for now ! Blind Obsession is not just high on emotions because it makes you questions what you are reading . But also high on steam and lust ! The sex in this book is scorchingly hot ! ( Is that even a word ?? ) Phillipe really knows how to get what he wants . And damn he dirty talks as well !! His feelings for Gemma were so confusing , that at times I just wanted to slap some sense into him .. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Do you always think about her?” Gemma asks, tearing him from his illusion. <br>“Yes,” he replies stoically. Gemma falls silent as her fingers stroke along his ribs and chest. <br>“Do you ever stop?” Phillipe squeezes his eyes shut, feeling his own deception mocking him. <br>“I stopped when I was inside of you.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/blindobsession2_zps557580d3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825781._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo blindobsession2_zps557580d3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m going to fuck you in a minute, Gemma, and it’s going to be hard.” He punctuates his sentence with another rough stroke. “If you don’t want that, then shut those sexy thighs and get the fuck out of here.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/blindobsession3_zps82bb4245.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825782.jpg" alt=" photo blindobsession3_zps82bb4245.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All the hot and sizzle were just burning up the pages .... FOR REALZ !!!<br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/oomph_zps6e677806.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380417470i/825783._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo oomph_zps6e677806.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But then , truth be told ! This book is just not about all the hot panties melting sex .. Its soo much more . Ella Frank manages to twist your emotions in a gut wrenching way . You know you don't want to like any of it . You know you don't want to understand any of it , and you sure as hell don't want it to happen . But her words and the way she has used it to mould this story will force to you like it , understand it and accept it ! <br><br>There were certain things that made me go , " Dude ,what the .... ??? " But I'm not getting into details with that one . The ending , again , tore me up completely . But I guess its not actually an ending . Its more like saying , ' anything can happen ... ' . Atleast that's how I see it .. <br><br>So what are you waiting for ?? Pick this book ASAP and read it . This one gets a 5 star from me just because I was stuck in my whirlwind of emotions . Blind Obsession is painstakingly haunting and beautifully crafted . It manages to fuck you in the head and leaves you satisfied in some morbid way that I have no answers to ... A must read for sure .. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1294.photobucket.com/user/Fufu_87/media/obs_zps731dfc80.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417470ra/825784.gif" alt=" photo obs_zps731dfc80.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>

<div id="review_592465698" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/592465698" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/592465698?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=i-like-it-dark-and-twisted">i-like-it-dark-and-twisted</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer592465698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14444285087436925040">Ella Frank orchestrated Blind Obsession to pull a reader into a world of art, music and mystery. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406894i/794307.jpg' width='381' height='225' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>
  <i>”When did it change from the story of two to the tragedy of three?”</i>
</b><br/><br/>This book was beautiful, sexually charged, profound, gripping, haunting and so well written!<br/><br/>As a reader, we follow Gemma Harris, a journalist to France for a career rocketing interview. She will uncover the <b>truth</b> about the relationship of the blind model/violinist Chantel Rosenberg and the gorgeous and much talked about artist, P</span>
  <span id="freeText14444285087436925040" style="display:none">Ella Frank orchestrated Blind Obsession to pull a reader into a world of art, music and mystery. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406894i/794307.jpg" width="381" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>”When did it change from the story of two to the tragedy of three?”</i>
</b><br><br>This book was beautiful, sexually charged, profound, gripping, haunting and so well written!<br><br>As a reader, we follow Gemma Harris, a journalist to France for a career rocketing interview. She will uncover the <b>truth</b> about the relationship of the blind model/violinist Chantel Rosenberg and the gorgeous and much talked about artist, Phillipe Tibideau.<br><br>Upon meeting Phillipe, (one of the most sexual, intense and tortured men I have read to date) Gemma is told that through Chantel’s secret journal and several interviews she will uncover the answers to the couple’s relationship as well as what events led to Chantel’s death.<br><br><b>Art</b>: Phillipe created The Blind Vision Collection. Which is a six piece collection of paintings modeled by Chantel Rosenberg, a blind violinist who many sources say was brainwashed by Phillipe.<br><br><b>Music</b>: Please see author’s page regularly to accompany your reading with the required music selections.<br><br><b>
  <i>”How can I be so fascinated with him and, at the same time, be so captivated by her?”</i>
</b><br><br>Through her steps of unraveling the story she becomes a part of the tale as much as the two main characters are. All the while love, beauty, pain and music play.<br><br><b>STOP THE RECAP!</b><br><br>This is where my description of the story will end. I’m not going to divulge what is uncovered. You MUST take the journey for yourself. Here’s why:<br><br>The writing…quotable and mesmerizing!<br><br><b>
  <i>”The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Love looks not with the eyes, but with the mind, and, therefore, is winged cupid blind.”</i>
</b><br><br>The sex…hot and abundant! Although, it never overshadowed the pain and beauty of the tale.<br><br>The ending won’t leave a reader with the usual they are expecting a baby, or a proposal story line. But things ended perfectly for me, once I gave my brain time to think of how other alternatives could have played out.<br><br>You will end up like me, <b>haunted</b> by Chantel, Phillipe and Gemma all the while hearing the most beautiful music your ears have ever heard.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Everything has beauty, but not everyone sees it.”</i>
</b><br><br>Bravo Ella Frank you have created a masterpiece!!!!!!<br><br><b>Final chapter in Philippe's POV</b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/final-impressions-phillipes-pov/">http://ellafrank30.wordpress.com/fina...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14444285087436925040" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16205457-shannon-the-show-stopper?shelf=always-a-keeper">always-a-keeper</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer601160319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17579062439474976728">A man in love with a woman....<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I love you. That is the beginning, and that is the end. That is everything."</i>
</b><br/><br/>A man so osbessed with her ghost....<br/><br/><a href='http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/_ghost_woman__by_nancy_long_ago-d53u19t_zps246df73e.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419236i/830929._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo _ghost_woman__by_nancy_long_ago-d53u19t_zps246df73e.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It leaves him unable to give himself to another....<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"When I was inside of her, nothing else existed," he confesses. <br/>"And when I'm inside you, she's starting not to exist."</i>
</b><br/><br/>This was such a haunting story that captivated me throughout. It's the most sensually erotic novel I've read and I will <i>never</i> look at a paintbrush again without having a stirr</span>
  <span id="freeText17579062439474976728" style="display:none">A man in love with a woman....<br><br><b>
  <i>"I love you. That is the beginning, and that is the end. That is everything."</i>
</b><br><br>A man so osbessed with her ghost....<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/_ghost_woman__by_nancy_long_ago-d53u19t_zps246df73e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419236i/830929._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo _ghost_woman__by_nancy_long_ago-d53u19t_zps246df73e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It leaves him unable to give himself to another....<br><br><b>
  <i>"When I was inside of her, nothing else existed," he confesses. <br>"And when I'm inside you, she's starting not to exist."</i>
</b><br><br>This was such a haunting story that captivated me throughout. It's the most sensually erotic novel I've read and I will <i>never</i> look at a paintbrush again without having a stirring deep within.<br><br><a href="http://s1341.photobucket.com/user/shannon_phillips6/media/Reviews/f445899716b9e8c1e8014c5c670_zps00f831b8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380419236i/830930._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo f445899716b9e8c1e8014c5c670_zps00f831b8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm gonna be honest, I didn't want it to end the way it did. I was able to accept it because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[of the painting Gemma received of herself with image of Chantel in the mirror. I felt like Phillipe was saying "I love you as much as I did her"  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><b>
  <i>"You can't break a man that's already broken."</i>
</b><br><br>I think some people are broken beyond repair and sadly, Phillipe is one of those people.<br><br>My first comment on this book before I even started was that I was going in blind. It's ironic, I had no clue one of the characters would be. If you like erotic romance, this book is <b>MUST</b> read. Another thing that sets this book apart from all other books is that it's two romances woven into one story and masterfully done at that. I didn't love one over the other....Just as Phillipe loved them both, so did I.<br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_476538987" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476538987" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476538987?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476538987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4416561150568026053">wow...... <br/><br/><b>4.75 STARS for this haunting and erotic tale.</b><br/><br/><b>Music...Art...Love....<i>Obsession</i></b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/solitary-kindle-addition.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188913._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo solitary-kindle-addition.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I know what you’re thinking… 4.75 stars… come on why not 5, well I’ll explain in a minute. First of all, I want to say how much I loved this story!!!! No, I mean I really <b>LOVED THIS STORY!!!!!!</b> This is the first novel I have read by Ella Frank, and I am very impressed. I have not read any of her contemporary romance novels, but I hear they are a bit different from this one. <br/><br/>First, and foremost,</span>
  <span id="freeText4416561150568026053" style="display:none">wow...... <br><br><b>4.75 STARS for this haunting and erotic tale.</b><br><br><b>Music...Art...Love....<i>Obsession</i></b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/solitary-kindle-addition.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188913._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo solitary-kindle-addition.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know what you’re thinking… 4.75 stars… come on why not 5, well I’ll explain in a minute. First of all, I want to say how much I loved this story!!!! No, I mean I really <b>LOVED THIS STORY!!!!!!</b> This is the first novel I have read by Ella Frank, and I am very impressed. I have not read any of her contemporary romance novels, but I hear they are a bit different from this one. <br><br>First, and foremost, I loved the way the story was presented. It was a contemporary romance…or tragedy if you want to get technical, but because of the nature of the circumstance surrounding the characters, the setting, and the affair that ensued, it could have occurred at any time. In fact, if there weren’t any references to the media and the internet mixed into the story, it would have been difficult to distinguish the period of time that the story took place.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/chateau-stairs.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188914.jpg" alt=" photo chateau-stairs.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“If there was obsession here— a dominant persistent desire— then it was the desire to lose ourselves in one another. The only problem is that one person is now lost, and the other is trapped.”<br></i>
</b><br>It was also told as a story within a story, with frequent flashbacks to certain events… in this case entries in a journal. This giving us a window into the mind of one of the main characters, one that has become even that much more intriguing in her death. <br>In addition, there was also an alternating POV, which I absolutely LOVE!!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>“Right now, you’re mine, just like she was mine. I’m going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can’t forget.”</i>
</b><br><br>This type of book always gives the reader a much better perspective into each character, a more accurate view of what is actually going on in the story. I love how the author intertwined their voices… Phillipe’s, Gemma’s and Chantel’s, to give the reader a better perspective as to what was going on in the story. <br><br>Now to the story…amazingly creative!!!! The use of art and music mixed together with a sensory disability…such as blindness was brilliant. Just the nature of art… being visual in nature and music, auditory, the author made it quite obvious that true vision, true sight, and true love are products of the mind and not the senses. Yes Chantel and Phillipe exploited physical love and sensuality through touch, but it was what was deeper, in their feelings, and in their hearts that made their love so untouchable. <br> <br><b>
  <i>When he originally went into this bargain with Gemma, he did it with the expectation that she would understand Chantel better, and as their story unraveled, she would get to see a side of him he found so difficult to show. He did not count on the intense feeling of connection to Chantel through Gemma. Perhaps it is Gemma herself? Maybe, if she didn’t seem so bewitched and curious about Chantel, he wouldn’t feel this way. Maybe if she just asked him questions in a perfunctory manner, he wouldn’t be feeling this aberrant entanglement of desire that he can’t seem to shake.</i>
</b><br><br>Then there was Gemma. It was hard to know who to pull for in this story. It was quite obvious how obsessive Phillipe’s love for Chantel was, but it was also not to want him to have love again in his life; and for Gemma, who was innocently caught within the story of their tragic loss. It was quite clear from the beginning that she would fall hard for our elusive Phillipe, but can we really expect him to move on after the tragedy he endured? Of course we do, because we are hopeless romantics who know that Chantel is gone, and would want him to be happy. But in reality, will he ever find a love so enrapturing again..? Probably not. But we can hope can’t we…that my friend is what sequels are for.<br><br><b>
  <i>I know I’m not the woman he so obviously hungers for and even though I’m not who he wants, I find myself stupidly willing to be her substitute.</i>
</b><br><br>My biggest reason for wanting to shout this story from the rooftops, and give it the highest possible rating was the ending… so I can’t elaborate, but I have to say, it ended the only way it could have, should have…true to its nature <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[tragic <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. That said I know many who would disagree with me. But once again…that is what sequels are for….dreamers.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ve fucking destroyed me. First, she did, and now, you are.”<br></i>
</b><br><br>So, now to the 0.25 stars I took off from the rating. I hate to even start on this topic, because I know I may be alone with the crickets on this subject, but here I go. <br>Now I know this could be considered erotica if you want to get technical, but I just found the sex a bit over-descriptive. And I really hate to nit-pick, but I’m just explaining my rating, that’s all. Too much talk about female arousal. There, I said it. Waaaaaaaay too much. I mean how wet can a woman get??? And how many ways can it be described? I just felt that this part of the story was way overdone. Too descriptive. And it really didn’t need it. The story was brilliant on its own. Not that I don’t enjoy a good sex scene, and let me tell you, Ella Frank KNOWS how to write a sex scene. I just got tired of the overly descriptive nature of it. That’s all.<br><br><b>
  <i>Les vrais paradis sont les paradis qu’on a perdus.<br>True paradises are paradises we have lost.</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/unnamed-kindle-edition.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188915._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo unnamed-kindle-edition.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But overall, FANTASTIC, INCREDIBLE, BEAUTIFUL STORY!!!!!!! And I loved the interactive nature of the book….with internet links to the art and music!!!! FABULOUS!!!!! Saved me lots of time looking things up!!!<br><br>I highly recommend this book!!! And I hope she considers a sequel… The characters were fabulous, and I hope to see more of their story in the future. <br><br>My character pics…<br><br><b>Phillipe Tibideaux<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/143783_id_BAh7CDoKc3R5bGUiIXdpZHRoOiA2MDBweDsgaGVpZ2h0OiA4MDBweDs6D3Jlc29sdXRpb25bB2kC1QFpAm4COgdpZGkDpzEC.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188916._SY540_.jpg" alt="Christian Jorgensen photo 143783_id_BAh7CDoKc3R5bGUiIXdpZHRoOiA2MDBweDsgaGVpZ2h0OiA4MDBweDs6D3Jlc29sdXRpb25bB2kC1QFpAm4COgdpZGkDpzEC.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Gemma Harris<br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/tumblr_m8pprt33411qz9qooo1_1280.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188917._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_m8pprt33411qz9qooo1_1280.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Chantel Rosenberg</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/AdriannaTateDuncan1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910503i/3188918.jpg" alt="Adrianna Tate Duncan photo AdriannaTateDuncan1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer597439080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer548400445050198466">UPDATE: I thought it would be interesting to go back and look at the very first review I ever posted on Goodreads. And this is STILL among my favorite books of all time. It is the only book that has ever made me cry. This is also the only book I have ever read that was interactive, meaning the text includes links to the music and art work featured in the story.<br/><br/>This book is a piece of art. <br/><br/>I still strongly recommend this book to fans of dark atmospheric stories. <br/> <br/>Reviewed on August, 23, 2013<br/>_____</span>
  <span id="freeText548400445050198466" style="display:none">UPDATE: I thought it would be interesting to go back and look at the very first review I ever posted on Goodreads. And this is STILL among my favorite books of all time. It is the only book that has ever made me cry. This is also the only book I have ever read that was interactive, meaning the text includes links to the music and art work featured in the story.<br /><br />This book is a piece of art. <br /><br />I still strongly recommend this book to fans of dark atmospheric stories. <br /> <br />Reviewed on August, 23, 2013<br />___________________________<br /><br />"....I'm going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can't forget."<br /><br />That's exactly what this book did to me. I read over 100 books a year and I have never felt the rollercoaster of emotions I felt while sinking in this dark and haunting story. It left me completely breathless and bawling my eyes out.<br /><br />Who are you Ella Frank?! ... and what have done to me?! .... and thank you for whatever it is! <br /><br />I don't leave reviews like.. ever! I'm only sharing my thoughts because I feel like not telling people would be a disservice to my fellow book addicts and to the author that has touched my soul with their words. <br /><br />Buy this book...don't borrow it...buy it. You will have to own it just as it will own you.</span>

<div id="review_540026420" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/540026420" />
    <a title="Desiree" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8261682-desiree"><img alt="Desiree" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/540026420?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

Talk about a roller coaster ride full of emotions. The Blind Obsession was a dark, twisted and slightly disturbing story leaving me with conflicting emotions.<br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/856/easy003.jpg/' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText10473740156659519171" style="display:none"><b>4.75/5 ☆ <u>Darkly Erotic Stars</u></b><br><br><b>Holy mindfuck.</b> Where do I begin... I really have no words for it. My mind is exhausted. Talk about a roller coaster ride full of emotions. The Blind Obsession was a dark, twisted and slightly disturbing story leaving me with conflicting emotions.<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/856/easy003.jpg/" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Renowned painter Phillipe Tibideau is best known for his exquisite collection of “The Blind Vision.” Phillipe is left feeling empty over his haunted past. Phillipe is intensely beyond obsessed with <b>her</b> all of his thoughts are consumed of her, only her, always her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410257i/804225.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_475402201" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/475402201" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/475402201?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=april-reads">april-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer475402201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14951607082885608311"> "The True Paradises are paradises we have Lost"<br/><br/>This story was brilliantly executed by Ella Frank. I found her writing to be flawless and beautiful from start to finish. The erotica in this book was some of the hottest I have ever read. While I read this story I was constantly intrigued as to what was "really" going on. I never really understood the full picture until the very end, and then it all came together beautifully. I certainly would not want to go into details about the story, as I feel</span>
  <span id="freeText14951607082885608311" style="display:none"> "The True Paradises are paradises we have Lost"<br /><br />This story was brilliantly executed by Ella Frank. I found her writing to be flawless and beautiful from start to finish. The erotica in this book was some of the hottest I have ever read. While I read this story I was constantly intrigued as to what was "really" going on. I never really understood the full picture until the very end, and then it all came together beautifully. I certainly would not want to go into details about the story, as I feel it is a mysterious journey that the reader must experience for themselves. I will say though that this story was haunting, and it is one that will be forever engraved in my head and heart. It touched me in a way that few stories do. This is a unique tale, and in todays book industry that is not an easy characteristic to find. <br />The basic story line begins with a journalist Gemma Harris) who goes to France, and the home of Phillipe Tibideau to get the full truth behind the man that people are calling "a beautiful monster." Phillipe has created "The Blind Vision Collection", which is a set of six sensual pictures he has painted that features the woman he essentially fell in love with. Chantal Rosenberg is an artist as well; but her trade is playing the violin. Chantal is a blind musician whose beauty and talent far surpass most, and she has captured Phillipe's heart and soul, in a way that he will never be the same.<br />Gemma has been invited by Phillipe to get to the bottom of what has happened in the lives of him and Chantal. The more that Gemma learns about these two talented and passionate people, the farther she begins to fall in love with both these souls. Desire between Phillipe and Gemma become something neither one can resist. Gemma falls further into Phillipes web; but truly Phillipe's heart is with someone else. Chantal has a hold on him that Gemma is desperately trying to understand. Will he be able to let go and give Gemma an honest chance, or will he remain a tormented soul who can not see past his obsession and love for Chantal.<br />Even though this book has a somewhat romantic tale to it, I would more classify it as a gothic romance. This is a tragic story in so many ways, and it is one that will leave you thinking long after it is done. I see Ella Frank going far as an author because she sure is able to write a wonderful story. I am just so impressed, and this book moved me to tears more than once. There are a few quotes that touched me:<br /><br />"You can't break a man who is already broken."<br /><br />"How do you give a tortured man absolution?"<br /><br />"The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision."<br /><br />"Love looks not with the eyes but with the mind.."<br /><br />I felt the need to add an additional comment about the book. I thought it was a refreshingly unique idea that Ella included links to the classical songs that were named in the book. This enriched the experience of reading this story and being able to have the music playing at the appropriate times in the book. She also included a visual aid, so that we could see what the paintings looked like of Chantal..This was a brilliant addition to the story and made it all the more richer because of it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14951607082885608311" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_491602861" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/491602861" />
    <a title="Mistress" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5511876-mistress"><img alt="Mistress" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383055853p2/5511876.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/491602861?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mistress" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mistress" href="/user/show/5511876-mistress">Mistress</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940016546674" href="/book/show/16382146-blind-obsession">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5511876-mistress?shelf=so-good">so-good</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer491602861" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16166598054746631658"><b><i>"Dreams and nightmares plagued him equally. It didn't matter which way the dream took him. Inevitably, when he awoke, one fact remained.</i> She <i>is gone."</i></b><br/><br/>WOW! The best way to describe this book for me is, <b> hauntingly beautiful </b>. Blind Obsession is one of a kind. I have never read anything like it, ever. The all-encompassing love and the utter tragedy of this story is absolutely heart wrenching. This is one of those books that you won't be able to forget. One that when you think back on it, will send</span>
  <span id="freeText16166598054746631658" style="display:none"><b><i>"Dreams and nightmares plagued him equally. It didn't matter which way the dream took him. Inevitably, when he awoke, one fact remained.</i> She <i>is gone."</i></b><br /><br />WOW! The best way to describe this book for me is, <b> hauntingly beautiful </b>. Blind Obsession is one of a kind. I have never read anything like it, ever. The all-encompassing love and the utter tragedy of this story is absolutely heart wrenching. This is one of those books that you won't be able to forget. One that when you think back on it, will send flashes of pain through your heart, while at the same time a small smile comes to your face. Most books have one great line that make you really pause and think, at its completion. Blind Obsession is filled with those heart-stopping lines from the beginning to the end. The brilliance that Ella Frank has written this story with is astounding. I love the music links and the pictures that are provided for an added experience while reading this book... again, completely original. I am amazed at how the past and present was written to flow together so seamlessly. The mystery in this story had me hanging onto every word I read. While reading this book I was swept away into a dark, seductive world as I listened to the music that <i>they</i> were listening to. I found myself seduced while reading <i>her</i> very private, detailed journal entries. With each page I was pulled further and deeper into this haunting tale. By the end, I thought my battered heart would completely shatter. I can't stress enough how badly this book deserves to be read. <b> Wow, just wow.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I'm struck with the realization that I'm holding onto a man who, for now, is holding onto me but he has still not let go of her."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Right now, you're mine, just like she was mine. I'm going to pull you under and drown you in me until you can't forget."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"He has a feeling that Gemma is the final act in this life, which he's already labeled a tragedy."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You are absolutely without question surreal, like a dream." As his breath washed over my face, he entreated, "God, don't ever let me wake."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I love you. That is the beginning, and that is the end. That is everything."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"The only thing worse than being blind is having sight but no vision."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Love looks not with the eyes but with the mind."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"The true paradises are paradises we have lost."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I will only be as far as your heart lets me go."</i>
</b><br /></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=brilliant-ending">brilliant-ending</a>,
