              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=mysterious">mysterious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=heartbreaking">heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=not-for-the-weak-hearted">not-for-the-weak-hearted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11644154-la-lionne?shelf=tough-ass-heroine">tough-ass-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer522413325" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16177580954306999550">Long overdue, but here it is...<br/><br/>**5 I-want-to-climb-into-this-book-and-live-in-it stars!**<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407545ra/796087.gif' width='400' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I don't think I have enough words in my vocabulary to write a review that will do this book justice.<br/>Usually, when I read a book, and I love it, I have a lot to say and can't wait to write the review. After I finished this one, I felt a bit differently. There are some books that makes you want to talk to someone, after you finish, about how great it was, and there are those that doesn't let go of you. You don</span>
  <span id="freeText16177580954306999550" style="display:none">Long overdue, but here it is...<br><br>**5 I-want-to-climb-into-this-book-and-live-in-it stars!**<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407545ra/796087.gif" width="400" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I don't think I have enough words in my vocabulary to write a review that will do this book justice.<br>Usually, when I read a book, and I love it, I have a lot to say and can't wait to write the review. After I finished this one, I felt a bit differently. There are some books that makes you want to talk to someone, after you finish, about how great it was, and there are those that doesn't let go of you. You don't want to talk to anyone or go back to the reality just yet. In my case it was the latter.<br><br>It's easier to pinpoint likes when there is something you didn't like. I loved everything about this story, every single chapter, every single sentence and characters in it. <br><br>Ah, Phillipe :-). He easily became one of my favorite characters of all times.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/545628._SX540_.gif" width="500" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Loner that lives in his bigass chateau, isolated himself from the word, trying to battle some demons that are haunting him.<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407545ra/796088.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I rarely get to read about such tortured characters. Readers don't get to know right away what kind of demons he's battling, but there is no mistake, something huge happened that completely destroyed him. He is not sure how to deal with it and where to go from here. How do you move on after something like that?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405145ra/788881.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gemma is a journalist. She comes to France to write an article about Phillipe, about what really happened. She wants to give him a chance to set the record straight.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407545i/796089._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Right away you see that she is way over her head, and that it won't be as easy as she thought, because Phillipe is a complicated character. She often gets frustrated, because he never gives her a straight answer. Sometimes she feels like he's talking in circles. He wants to tell her the whole story, but he chooses a very unconventional way to teach her about him and what really happened.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Phillipe knows she is uncomfortable. I'll be damned if I'm going to ease her. If she wants to go down this rabbit hole with him, then she better be prepared for what she will find."</i>
</b><br><br>Very quickly she gets completely lost in him. Their passion is through the roof. It's like a wild fire. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403710i/785464.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Passion, it lies in all of us, sleeping... waiting... and though unwanted... unbidden... it will stir... open its jaws and howl. It speaks to us... guides us... passion rules us all, and we obey. What other choice do we have? Passion is the source of our finest moments. The joy of love... the clarity of hatred... and the ecstasy of grief. It hurts sometimes more than we can bear. If we could live without passion maybe we'd know some kind of peace... but we would be hollow... Empty rooms shuttered and dank. Without passion we'd be truly dead”<br><br>- Joss Whedon -</b>
</blockquote><br>But as grate as their sex is, she still wants answers, she wants to understand him. She feels frustrated, and at times angry. She feels like he is not trusting her and not being completely honest with her. She decides to leave...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407545ra/796090.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But every time she tries to leave, he pulls her right back in. He doesn't want her there, because he feels she's getting to close to the edge of the rabithole. But at the same time, he can't seem to let her go. They are pushing each other to the limit, tho the point of no return. What will she do when she discovers the truth?<br><br> <b>"There's a part of you, Gemma, that's so fucking sweet, and I want to steal that part of you, even though I know I shouldn't."</b><br>***<br><b>"My needy body is responding to every word he's saying while my mind is screaming at me to get out of here. It's telling me over and over that he's playing with me, yet my weeping sex is yelling at me to shut the hell up and let him have me."</b><br><br>As she gets closer to the truth, she feels like the very same demon that haunts Phillipe, start haunting her too. But she doesn't want to run from it, she is fascinated and mesmerized by "it". She gets it now, why it's so hard for him to let it go... It's very painful to read about them drowning in each others sorrows. <br><br>The ending was absolutely brilliant. It left me with more questions than I had when I started the book. Very suiting ending to such an intense story. <br><br><b>"The harder you love, the harder you fall<br>Everything or nothing at all<br>The more you can take, the harder you break"<br><br>- Unknown -</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399784ra/774014.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380407545ra/796091.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is an amazing piece of literature. Superbly written and an absolute page turner that will stay with me for a long long time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16177580954306999550" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer585747866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10556856793126112490">There are really not enough stars on GR to rate this book! Even if the rating was out of ten, this book would qualify for eleven and then some ...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416956ra/824079.gif' alt=' photo icantstopthinkingaboutit_zps74baf606.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Have you ever read a book, seen a movie, heard a story, etc. that moved you so much that you just knew it will haunt you for a very long time, if not for the rest of your life?? And have you ever wished that said book, movie, story, etc. had a different ending to the point that every time you read it, seen it or heard it again, you closed your eyes tow</span>
  <span id="freeText10556856793126112490" style="display:none">There are really not enough stars on GR to rate this book! Even if the rating was out of ten, this book would qualify for eleven and then some ...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416956ra/824079.gif" alt=" photo icantstopthinkingaboutit_zps74baf606.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Have you ever read a book, seen a movie, heard a story, etc. that moved you so much that you just knew it will haunt you for a very long time, if not for the rest of your life?? And have you ever wished that said book, movie, story, etc. had a different ending to the point that every time you read it, seen it or heard it again, you closed your eyes towards the end and tried to will for it to happen?<br><br>Well ... this is one of those books for me.<br><br>To say that I am an emotional mess right now would be a colossal understatement. I haven't been moved by a story/book this much in a very long time. <br><br>Three different POVs concept by the author was absolutely brilliant! It made the characters seem that much more real. <br><br>Even though your heart breaks as you read their story, you can't help but think how lucky Chantel and Phillipe really were to have experienced this kind of love for one another. I guess you can't help but agree with whoever said "better to have loved and lost than never to have loved at all". What they shared, even though for just a short period of time, was truly special and you envy this kind of love ... one can all only dream of having this type of connection with another human being.<br><br>When I read Phillipe's recollection of that fateful day, my heart was aching for him. Are you ever able to move on after such tragedy?<br><br>And, if you were Gemma, would you ever recover if something like this were to happen to you?<br><br>The ending wasn't your typical HEA ending, however, when you really think about it, both characters did get some closure in a way ... <br><br>The last chapter in Phillipe's POV (bonus chapter on Ella's site) was brilliant and gave me hope that, maybe in time, Phillipe will be able to move on.<br><br>In order to get a full on emotional experience while reading this, try playing suggested playlist at appropriate times. Just when you thoughts you couldn't cry any more ... <br><br><br>Ironically, Air by Bach is one of my favorite classical pieces that I will never be able to listen to again without shedding a tear.<br><br><br>ETA: I applaud Ella's decision [as much as I would have LOVED to revist these characters in the future] to not write a sequel for this perfection!</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Ella Frank Fans, Romance</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer715721056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3347126217199546274"><b>4.5 Emotional, Thought Provoking, Life-Affirming, and Intoxicating Stars<br/>* * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free- A 2013 Review</i><br/>This book was highly recommended to me by Jahy and Irene. Because of them, I have experienced a story of love which can overtake one’s mind, body and soul.</b> It can make a person become more than they ever thought they could; do things which they never intended and give of themselves to the desire to heal another more than protect their heart. <br/><br/>This story is told from three points of view;</span>
  <span id="freeText3347126217199546274" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Emotional, Thought Provoking, Life-Affirming, and Intoxicating Stars<br>* * * * 1/2 <i>Spoiler Free- A 2013 Review</i><br>This book was highly recommended to me by Jahy and Irene. Because of them, I have experienced a story of love which can overtake one’s mind, body and soul.</b> It can make a person become more than they ever thought they could; do things which they never intended and give of themselves to the desire to heal another more than protect their heart. <br><br>This story is told from three points of view; with each bringing so much to the reader.<br><br>As someone who is new to reviewing, I highly recommend you read more detailed, insightful descriptions than mine. <br><br>What I can share is if you put yourself totally into this story, experiencing everything as the author intends freely, then you will not be disappointed.<br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UBkROxcc/2O/Iy1CYYd1rG3tTIFrNDYD5Fmpp1xVIqnNhPSBP8RAT5hYtbVKUU+i9Yzwv/pI2WwrA+qIfz7VXQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HfHxvoeaXwbYzMB8RgoUbUORMAFV6b5iOE4l07SFnw6AbBQEr0LgKv+3WItt3C5j2/CMP8SVUQ33FGb8l+5o+g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer17238230501519043250">Ella Frank is the USA Today Bestselling Author of the Temptation series, including Try, Take, and Trust and is the co-author of the fan-favorite erotic serial, Sex Addict. <br/><br/>A life-long fan of the romance genre, Ella writes contemporary and erotic fiction. </span>
